             <script>
              $(document).ready(function() {
  hpResizeRecentStories();
});

$(window).on("orientationchange",function(){
  hpResizeRecentStories();
});

function hpResizeRecentStories() {
  var maxSeactionFeatureHeight = 200;

  jQuery('.section-feature-article article').each(function() {
    if ($(this).height() > maxSeactionFeatureHeight) {
      maxSeactionFeatureHeight = $(this).height();
    }
  
    $(this).addClass('section-feature-article-wrapper');
  });
   
  //jQuery('.section-feature-article-wrapper').height(maxSeactionFeatureHeight + 'px');

  var maxArticleHeight = 100;

  jQuery('.recent-posts-content').each(function() {
    if ($(this).height() > maxArticleHeight) {
      maxArticleHeight = $(this).height();
    }
  
    $(this).addClass('recent-article-wrapper');
  });

  jQuery('.recent-posts-content').height(maxArticleHeight + 'px');
}
             </script>
